This absolutely was “The Breakfast Club Meets Pretty Little Liars.” Per usual, I was not the target audience for this selection, but hey the sun shines on an old dog’s butt every once in a while because I thought it was . . . . <br><br><a href="http://lunapic.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1487786334ra/22051188.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I suspect <i>One Of Us Is Lying</i> will become a bestseller P.D.Q. (that’s pretty darn quick for you young’ins) and I wouldn’t be surprised to see it optioned as a movie in the not-so-distant future either. If you read mysteries . . . like ever . . . . you'll probably see the end coming about 12 miles away, but the getting there is all the fun. Obviously this isn't a story that’s going to change anyone’s lives, but if you have a teen (or in my case a 30 year old male attorney boss) who enjoys all the guilty pleasures <i>Pretty Little Liars</i> has to offer on the ABC Family Channel, this will probably be a winner.<br><br><i>ARC provided by NetGalley in exchange for an honest review. <div id="review_2651701514" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2651701514" />
    <a title="✨ A ✨ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/65321843-a"><img alt="✨ A ✨ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1604503440p2/65321843.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2651701514?book_show_action=true">Jan 20, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✨ A ✨ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="✨ A ✨ " href="/user/show/65321843-a">✨ A ✨ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/65321843-a?shelf=read-in-2019">read-in-2019</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/65321843-a?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/65321843-a?shelf=four-and-half-stars">four-and-half-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/65321843-a?shelf=mystery-thriller">mystery-thriller</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/65321843-a?shelf=faves-ya-mystery">faves-ya-mystery</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2651701514" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer779302263685972209">It's been a while since I've read a good YA mystery. And gosh am I glad that I finally picked this one up. <br/><br/>First chapter and <i>BOOM!</i> I was sucked in. <br/><br/><b>What I loved:</b><br/>• the mystery and suspense element was top notch 👌. <br/>• the characters were so interesting to read about. At first they all seemed to fit their respective labels - the geek; the princess; the golden boy and the badboy criminal. Pretty straight forward right? But delving into each of their lives we see that there is more to each of them. An</span>
  <span id="freeText779302263685972209" style="display:none">It's been a while since I've read a good YA mystery. And gosh am I glad that I finally picked this one up. <br /><br />First chapter and <i>BOOM!</i> I was sucked in. <br /><br /><b>What I loved:</b><br />• the mystery and suspense element was top notch 👌. <br />• the characters were so interesting to read about. At first they all seemed to fit their respective labels - the geek; the princess; the golden boy and the badboy criminal. Pretty straight forward right? But delving into each of their lives we see that there is more to each of them. And they all had secrets. <br />• the writing and the pacing had me feeling like I was binge watching an addictive Netflix series. If that's not an indicator of a good book then I don't know what is. <br />• I love me a good sibling bond in a book. Recently I've been reading books where there is sibling hate or no siblings at all. Personally I have five siblings - not that we all get along all the time. But I feel like sibling relationships don't get enough rep and are unappreciated.<br /><br /><br />Even though I figured out the twist I still think the above reasons is what made this book so good. <br /><br />I am so glad to know that there will be a <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2681868157" rel="nofollow noopener">sequel</a> to come, because gosh I need more of these amazing characters and when I got to the last page I was sad to let them go. 😔</span>
  <a data-text-id="779302263685972209" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText9404869699845463100" style="display:none">You had me at.... it starts out like The Breakfast Club...I mean yes! Bring it on. Now I am left wondering what took me so long to pick up this book. I loved it. I think I was hesitate to read it due to it being classified as YA and I really have not read many YA. That might have to change! <br /><br />Bayview High...detention...be there! The Breakfast Club vibe is strong when we start out with a rather unlikely group of kids meeting for detention. This is not your typical bunch of kids that frequent such punishments, in fact I think only one of them has had this joyful experience and that is Nate. I loved how the students were classified into their "groups" they associated with. The beauty, the brain, the criminal and the athlete...I mean we all know these groups really do exist in high school. <br /><br />What did I love most? As a thriller genre reader, this book was a breath of fresh air. It had such a unique storyline and honestly I did not guess the ending. I had no idea who was to blame for only 4 students making it out alive! Everyone had a reason to want Simon silenced, but who actually silenced him forever?!!<br /><br />I never thought I was a YA kind of girl but I guess I am 🤷‍♀️I really enjoyed this book ❤️Looking forward to One Of Us Is Next !</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer11614853747206849812">detective jessica, human lie detector, reporting for duty!<br/><br/>i got to the bottom of this and figured it out pretty easily early on, but that didnt detract from the story in the slightest. initially, i was worried this was going to be too much like the breakfast club meets murder she wrote but, other than the student stereotypes, this wasnt like that at all and i was so glad.<br/><br/>i loved how entertaining this was. i appreciated the little twists and turns, here and there, that kept me on my toes whilst i</span>
  <span id="freeText11614853747206849812" style="display:none">detective jessica, human lie detector, reporting for duty!<br /><br />i got to the bottom of this and figured it out pretty easily early on, but that didnt detract from the story in the slightest. initially, i was worried this was going to be too much like the breakfast club meets murder she wrote but, other than the student stereotypes, this wasnt like that at all and i was so glad.<br /><br />i loved how entertaining this was. i appreciated the little twists and turns, here and there, that kept me on my toes whilst i was so focused on the big end reveal. i also thought this was especially impressive for a debut - stories like this are pretty common, so it quite ambitious to try to make it your own, but i thought mcmanus nailed this. it had great pacing, solid writing, an engaging plot, and interesting characters. and i also now have a new book boyfriend in the form of nate, so thats always a bonus! <br /><br />i cant wait to see what kind of books mcmanus writes next! hopefully its more of this, please and thank you!<br /><br /><b>↠ <i>4 stars</i></b></span>

<div id="review_2078560811" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2078560811" />
    <a title="Misstdennis" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/41744660-misstdennis"><img alt="Misstdennis" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1570069040p2/41744660.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2078560811?book_show_action=true">Aug 17, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Misstdennis" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Misstdennis" href="/user/show/41744660-misstdennis">Misstdennis</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780141375632" href="/book/show/32887579-one-of-us-is-lying">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41744660-misstdennis?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41744660-misstdennis?shelf=owned-books">owned-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2078560811" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12855432620734586585"><b> 5 Stars!</b><br/><br/><i>“Unless one of us is lying. Which is always a possibility.”</i><br/><br/>Oh me oh my, this book was not what I expected at all.<br/>I hadn't looked into the plot too much so I was going in half blind in a way.<br/>I was thinking this would be <b>The Breakfast Club 2.0</b>. <br/><i>But I was wrong.</i><br/>I thought this was going to be yet <b>another YA Contemporary novel with predictable plots</b>.<br/><i>But I was wrong.</i><br/><br/>This book was so gripping and I flew through the pages like it was no tomorrow.<br/>From start to finish I was on the edge of my seat</span>
  <span id="freeText12855432620734586585" style="display:none"><b> 5 Stars!</b><br><br><i>“Unless one of us is lying. Which is always a possibility.”</i><br><br>Oh me oh my, this book was not what I expected at all.<br>I hadn't looked into the plot too much so I was going in half blind in a way.<br>I was thinking this would be <b>The Breakfast Club 2.0</b>. <br><i>But I was wrong.</i><br>I thought this was going to be yet <b>another YA Contemporary novel with predictable plots</b>.<br><i>But I was wrong.</i><br><br>This book was so gripping and I flew through the pages like it was no tomorrow.<br>From start to finish I was on the edge of my seat and trying to figure out the murder like a was on an episode of Law and Order.<br>And if I'm going to toot my own horn here, I figured out who the culprit was around the half way mark.<br><i>Detective Taylor, at your service. </i><br>But in saying that, the way the plot was constructed still left me surprised by the end of the book.<br><i>So sneaky...</i><br><br>I will mention that this story heavily focuses around <b>harassment</b>, <b>mental abuse</b> and <b>homophobia</b>.<br>So if you're quite sensitive around these topics, just be mindful. <br><br>I try and make all my reviews <b>spoiler free</b> as it's just easier for review purposes <i>(who am I kidding? I'm just lazy lol)</i> So I won't go into too much detail.<br>But the story focuses heavily on 4 Students:<br><b>Bronwyn</b>, <b>Cooper</b>, <b>Nate</b> and <b>Addy</b>. And like the Breakfast club, they are all completely different students but unlike The Breakfast Club, they turn to each other for support because they have all been involved in a murder they have just witnessed together.<br>And let me just say, these students were so fantastic.<br><br><i>“I guess we're almost friends now, or as friendly as you can get when you're not one hundred percent sure the other person isn't framing you for murder.” </i><br><br>I really connected with them and my heart got heavy for them in so many ways.<br>I was angry, upset, excited and felt that I was going to burst into confetti at any given moment.<br><br>I think <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/15127507.Karen_M__McManus" title="Karen M. McManus" rel="nofollow noopener">Karen M. McManus</a> did a fantastic job with this book.<br>The style of writing, the plot with all the twist and turns that left me guessing in most parts, was just <b>SO GOOD MAN!</b><br>Kudos to you, Karen! <br><br>I'll be thinking about this book <i>(especially the ending because fuck man, I almost died. Twice.)</i> and will pick this book up again in the future.<br>So if you're yet to read this and in the mood for a bit of teenage mystery. Pick it up. You'll thank me later...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1482557082ra/21527613.gif" width="400" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="12855432620734586585" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_2447042255" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2447042255" />
    <a title="BernLuvsBooks " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3087404-bernluvsbooks"><img alt="BernLuvsBooks " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1585010050p2/3087404.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2447042255?book_show_action=true">Jul 13, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="BernLuvsBooks " class="user" itemprop="url" name="BernLuvsBooks " href="/user/show/3087404-bernluvsbooks">BernLuvsBooks </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3087404-bernluvsbooks?shelf=2018">2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3087404-bernluvsbooks?shelf=adult-reads">adult-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2447042255" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10751022563659121122"><b> 5 Students walk into detention. A few minutes later 1 of them is dead. </b> <b> <i> Who killed Simon? </i></b> <br/><br/>I've been wanting to read <b> <u> <i> One of Us is Lying </i></u></b>   for awhile now. I am a hug fan of tv shows like Riverdale and Pretty Little Liars and teen movies like Breakfast Club, Sixteen Candles, Mean Girls, Can't Buy Me Love, Scream, etc. I could go on & on. It's pretty bad - I can't flip through the channels and see any of those on without watching. Therefore, it's no surprise that this book seemed like a perf</span>
  <span id="freeText10751022563659121122" style="display:none"><b> 5 Students walk into detention. A few minutes later 1 of them is dead. </b> <b> <i> Who killed Simon? </i></b> <br /><br />I've been wanting to read <b> <u> <i> One of Us is Lying </i></u></b>   for awhile now. I am a hug fan of tv shows like Riverdale and Pretty Little Liars and teen movies like Breakfast Club, Sixteen Candles, Mean Girls, Can't Buy Me Love, Scream, etc. I could go on &amp; on. It's pretty bad - I can't flip through the channels and see any of those on without watching. Therefore, it's no surprise that this book seemed like a perfect fit for me. I'm not even sure why it took me this long to read it. <br /><br /><b> <u> <i> One of Us is Lying </i></u></b>   isn't a very complex mystery. I had it figured out from the beginning. Well, admittedly I can't say I had all the angles completely figured out but the main twist - I called it right from Ch.1. Usually, that would ruin things for me but this time I didn't even mind it. I knew what I was getting into with this YA mystery and I was definitely along for the entire ride. ;) <br /><br /><b> This book was better than a daytime soap opera! </b>Seriously, EVERYONE was lying or hiding something from everyone else. Yet, I genuinely cared about these kids. These 4 SUSPECTS - they captured my heart. I loved how they grew throughout the story. Addy - who I found spineless and whiny in the beginning completely won me over by the end. I was literally cheering her on - OUT LOUD! Nate - who doesn't love the misunderstood, brooding bad boy rebel! What's not to love about sweet as Pie Cooper? Finally, Bronwyn a.k.a Miss Goody-two-shoes reminded me of me. Obviously she was my fave! I enjoyed watching these 4 form an unlikely alliance and band together to figure out what really happened. <br /><br />Here's the thing - even though I had the whodunnit mostly figured out, there was a twist that I hadn't seen coming. That made reading the book even better than I initially expected. Is the book a bit cliche? Yes, but that's what makes it fun &amp; a bit nostalgic. Does it depend on stereotypical characters? Yes, but don't they often do that? I felt like these characters showed growth from beginning to end which you don't often get to see in YA mysteries. What some might see as negatives I saw as positives for this book. It was fun, nostalgic, engaging and extremely readable. It held my interest from beginning to end.</span>
  <a data-text-id="10751022563659121122" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2179704353" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2179704353" />
    <a title="emma" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/32879029-emma"><img alt="emma" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1520568130p2/32879029.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2179704353?book_show_action=true">Nov 09, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="emma" class="user" itemprop="url" name="emma" href="/user/show/32879029-emma">emma</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32879029-emma?shelf=eh">eh</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32879029-emma?shelf=dark">dark</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32879029-emma?shelf=diverse">diverse</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32879029-emma?shelf=3-stars">3-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32879029-emma?shelf=mystery-thriller-horror-etc">mystery-thriller-horror-etc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32879029-emma?shelf=ya">ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32879029-emma?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2179704353" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13659602894429711245">Recently, I started watching How to Get Away with Murder. Because I am totally untrendy and if by some trick of nature I am somehow participating in something that people at large appreciate, I must do so four years too late in order to keep the world running and not break fundamental laws of world operation, probably.<br/><br/>It’s a very entertaining show! Twisty and turny. Very dark. I’ve gasped a few times. Viola Davis is a national treasure.<br/><br/>That show is a lot better than this book.<br/><br/>It, like this book,</span>
  <span id="freeText13659602894429711245" style="display:none">Recently, I started watching How to Get Away with Murder. Because I am totally untrendy and if by some trick of nature I am somehow participating in something that people at large appreciate, I must do so four years too late in order to keep the world running and not break fundamental laws of world operation, probably.<br /><br />It’s a very entertaining show! Twisty and turny. Very dark. I’ve gasped a few times. Viola Davis is a national treasure.<br /><br />That show is a lot better than this book.<br /><br />It, like this book, follows a group of young people and a murder, and mystery surrounding that murder. It, too, involves steamy romance and social media and endless drama.<br /><br />But it’s just totally, full-on better at doing all of it. There’s no avoiding it.<br /><br />That’s not to say that this book isn’t good! It is. Or at least it isn’t bad.<br /><br />Here’s the thing. It’s the watered-down, YA version of How to Get Away with Murder. Some people prefer those versions! And that’s okay.<br /><br />If you liked Warcross better than Ready Player One. If you’re more interested in Pretty Little Liars and Riverdale than Mindhunter or Making a Murderer. It’s fine if you are! They’re just two totally different things.<br /><br />YA murder stuff is frothier. There are YA requisites it has to meet: budding romance; groups of friends; high school drama; usually some sort of impending-future college-slash-career-goals plotline.<br /><br />It all depends if you want a side of fluff with your murder mystery.<br /><br />I, personally, don’t. Give me darkness and thrills and creeps and gore. Do not give me baseball drama and romantic miscommunication and phones getting taken away, please. I’m not interested.<br /><br />But as far as that goes, this book was pretty good at it. It, at the very least, incorporated the drama into the murder and the motive. <br /><br />The ending was predictable, yes, and sort of messy really, and definitely not creepy or shocking or the things I really want, but it was unique and somewhat creative.<br /><br />This whole shindig, actually, was much more unique and creative than I expected. I really didn’t <i>not</i> enjoy it, even though I’ve been so busy trying to lock down the “Most Pretentious Person Alive” award while writing this that I may not have had the time to convey that.<br /><br />I think it’s that I just finished You by Caroline Kepnes. And that’s really just a much better book than this. Unfair standard, though. <br /><br />Bottom line: If you want young adult sh*t in your thriller and not just thrills, this book is perfect for you. If you’re here for the thrills, there are way, way, way better choices.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13659602894429711245" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

			<a class="actionLink" href="/topic/show/21045024-can-we-all-agree-this-should-become-a-movie">Can we all agree this should become a movie?</a>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('pxnY2fUvhwVQWS4I29OJyk6sOvrbOI0M71D90cWhYC+dP7ELTnFObfdymmksJoMVmPPdMhW1A2u0LrtgCOKStQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('mj2GwOY5isW3duqnRghezLXfcR7XQs3Nw9uOPT2RuOagG+8SXWdDrRBdXsax/VQTY4CW1hnPQ6qYpciM8NJKfA==')})
  }
